You await my return, sitting sleepless near a cradle,

general 2020-08-26 00:47:01 224jay's guide on how to: search & destroy undes
(Comes from my experiences)

1. Identifying unde
You can suspect users who applies to these standards as an unde:
- uses image of their roblox / minecraft character for pfp.
- shitty builds, high ego.
- often spams "XD" unironically.
- mostly unranked.
- has "YT", "Gaming", "TV" in their username.
- frequent grammar mistakes.

2. Checking their real age.
 The suspected "unde" user can be either an actual unde, or a manchild with a mental age of 7 year old's.
You can either:
-Pursue them to send screenshot of birthday set in settings > account info.
About 50% of them will send it, and other half will most likely refuse sending it, saying you're not a mod and you have no perms to ask for an info.
You can either:
-continue pursuing.
-ping the chat moderators, and ask them to pursue instead. (There is high chance of chat moderators ignoring it, but once they start pursuing, things will go much easier.)

3. Result
-If the user turns out to be an unde: grab popcorn, ping mod, watch them undes vanish to outer space.
-If the user turns out to be 13+ manchild: it do be bruh moment doe.
-If the user refuses sending screenshot and chat mods ignore it: Yeah. Worst scenario.
